001|# Systematic Approach to Handle Intermediate-Level Coding Challenges
002|
003|## Language & Project Info
004|- **Language:** English
005|- **Programming Language:** Python, JavaScript/React
006|- **Project Name:** systematic_coding_challenges
007|- **Original Requirements:** Create a systematic approach to handle intermediate-level coding challenges in Python, JavaScript/React, and database design, ensuring fully functional code that includes thorough documentation.
008|
009|## Product Definition
010|### Product Goals
011|1. Develop a structured framework for solving coding challenges.
012|2. Ensure all code is functional and well-documented.
013|3. Maintain a consistent turnaround time for challenge completion.
014|
015|### User Stories
016|- As a developer, I want a clear framework for tackling coding challenges so that I can improve my problem-solving skills.
017|- As a team lead, I want to ensure that all code submissions are well-documented so that they can be easily understood by others.
018|- As a project manager, I want to track the turnaround time for coding challenges to ensure efficiency in our workflow.
019|### Competitive Analysis
020|- **Competitor 1: LeetCode**
021|  - **Pros:** Extensive problem set, community solutions, and discussions.
022|  - **Cons:** Limited documentation support for solutions.
023|- **Competitor 2: HackerRank**
024|  - **Pros:** Structured challenges, company-specific assessments.
025|  - **Cons:** Less focus on documentation and code quality.
026|- **Competitor 3: Codewars**
027|  - **Pros:** Gamified learning experience, community-driven challenges.
028|  - **Cons:** Inconsistent quality of challenges.
029|- **Competitor 4: Exercism**
030|  - **Pros:** Focus on mentorship and code reviews.
031|  - **Cons:** Limited language support compared to others.
032|- **Competitor 5: Codecademy**
033|  - **Pros:** Interactive learning environment, beginner-friendly.
034|  - **Cons:** Less emphasis on intermediate-level challenges.

001|# Systematic Approach to Handle Intermediate-Level Coding Challenges
002|
003|## Language & Project Info
004|- **Language:** English
005|- **Programming Language:** Python, JavaScript/React
006|- **Project Name:** systematic_coding_challenges
007|- **Original Requirements:** Create a systematic approach to handle intermediate-level coding challenges in Python, JavaScript/React, and database design, ensuring fully functional code that includes thorough documentation.
008|
009|## Product Definition
010|### Product Goals
011|1. Develop a structured framework for solving coding challenges.
012|2. Ensure all code is functional and well-documented.
013|3. Maintain a consistent turnaround time for challenge completion.
014|
015|### User Stories
016|- As a developer, I want a clear framework for tackling coding challenges so that I can improve my problem-solving skills.
017|- As a team lead, I want to ensure that all code submissions are well-documented so that they can be easily understood by others.
018|- As a project manager, I want to track the turnaround time for coding challenges to ensure efficiency in our workflow.
019|### Competitive Analysis
020|- **Competitor 1: LeetCode**
021|  - **Pros:** Extensive problem set, community solutions, and discussions.
022|  - **Cons:** Limited documentation support for solutions.
023|- **Competitor 2: HackerRank**

005|- **Programming Language:** Python, JavaScript/React
006|- **Project Name:** systematic_coding_challenges

009|## Product Definition
010|### Product Goals
011|1. Develop a structured framework for solving coding challenges.
012|2. Ensure all code is functional and well-documented.
013|3. Maintain a consistent turnaround time for challenge completion.
014|
015|### User Stories
016|- As a developer, I want a clear framework for tackling coding challenges so that I can improve my problem-solving skills.
017|- As a team lead, I want to ensure that all code submissions are well-documented so that they can be easily understood by others.
018|- As a project manager, I want to track the turnaround time for coding challenges to ensure efficiency in our workflow.

020|- **Competitor 1: LeetCode**

022|  - **Cons:** Limited documentation support for solutions.
023|- **Competitor 2: HackerRank**
024|  - **Pros:** Structured challenges, company-specific assessments.
025|  - **Cons:** Less focus on documentation and code quality.
026|- **Competitor 3: Codewars**
027|  - **Pros:** Gamified learning experience, community-driven challenges.
028|  - **Cons:** Inconsistent quality of challenges.
029|- **Competitor 4: Exercism**
030|  - **Pros:** Focus on mentorship and code reviews.
031|  - **Cons:** Limited language support compared to others.
032|- **Competitor 5: Codecademy**
033|  - **Pros:** Interactive learning environment, beginner-friendly.
034|  - **Cons:** Less emphasis on intermediate-level challenges.
035|### Requirements Analysis
036|- A structured framework for coding challenges that includes problem-solving strategies.
037|- Documentation standards for code submissions to ensure clarity and maintainability.
038|- Tools and resources for tracking turnaround times and performance metrics.

040|- **P0: Must-have requirements**
041|  - A structured framework for coding challenges.
042|  - Documentation standards for code submissions.

001|# Systematic Approach to Handle Intermediate-Level Coding Challenges
002|
003|## Language & Project Info
004|- **Language:** English
005|- **Programming Language:** Python, JavaScript/React
006|- **Project Name:** systematic_coding_challenges
007|- **Original Requirements:** Create a systematic approach to handle intermediate-level coding challenges in Python, JavaScript/React, and database design, ensuring fully functional code that includes thorough documentation.
008|
009|## Product Definition
010|### Product Goals
011|1. Develop a structured framework for solving coding challenges.
012|2. Ensure all code is functional and well-documented.
013|3. Maintain a consistent turnaround time for challenge completion.
014|
015|### User Stories
016|- As a developer, I want a clear framework for tackling coding challenges so that I can improve my problem-solving skills.
017|- As a team lead, I want to ensure that all code submissions are well-documented so that they can be easily understood by others.
018|- As a project manager, I want to track the turnaround time for coding challenges to ensure efficiency in our workflow.
019|### Competitive Analysis
020|- **Competitor 1: LeetCode**
021|  - **Pros:** Extensive problem set, community solutions, and discussions.
022|  - **Cons:** Limited documentation support for solutions.
023|- **Competitor 2: HackerRank**
024|  - **Pros:** Structured challenges, company-specific assessments.
025|  - **Cons:** Less focus on documentation and code quality.
026|- **Competitor 3: Codewars**
027|  - **Pros:** Gamified learning experience, community-driven challenges.
028|  - **Cons:** Inconsistent quality of challenges.
029|- **Competitor 4: Exercism**
030|  - **Pros:** Focus on mentorship and code reviews.
031|  - **Cons:** Limited language support compared to others.
032|- **Competitor 5: Codecademy**
033|  - **Pros:** Interactive learning environment, beginner-friendly.
034|  - **Cons:** Less emphasis on intermediate-level challenges.
035|### Requirements Analysis
036|- A structured framework for coding challenges that includes problem-solving strategies.
037|- Documentation standards for code submissions to ensure clarity and maintainability.
038|- Tools and resources for tracking turnaround times and performance metrics.
039|### Requirements Pool
040|- **P0: Must-have requirements**
041|  - A structured framework for coding challenges.
042|  - Documentation standards for code submissions.
043|- **P1: Should-have requirements**
044|  - Tools for tracking turnaround times.
045|- **P2: Nice-to-have requirements**
046|  - Performance metrics analysis tools.
047|### UI Design Draft
048|- **Dashboard:** A user-friendly interface displaying available coding challenges with filters for difficulty and language.
049|- **Submission Area:** A dedicated section for users to submit their solutions, including options for code review and feedback.
050|- **Documentation Section:** An accessible area for coding standards, best practices, and guidelines to ensure well-documented submissions.
051|### Open Questions
052|- What specific metrics will be used to track turnaround times?
053|- Are there any preferred tools or platforms for implementing the framework?
054|- How will user feedback be collected and integrated into the system?
